 39 | function isAllowedExternalLink(url: string): boolean {
 40 |   try {
 41 |     const parsed = new URL(url);
 42 |     return parsed.protocol === "https:" && EXTERNAL_LINK_HOSTS.has(parsed.hostname);
 43 |   } catch {
 44 |     return false;
 45 |   }
 46 | }

 48 | function openAllowedExternalLink(url: string): void {
 49 |   if (isAllowedExternalLink(url)) {
 50 |     void shell.openExternal(url);
 51 |   }
 52 | }

103 | function createGitWorker(): UtilityProcess {
104 |   const worker = utilityProcess.fork(path.join(__dirname, "workers", "git-worker.js"));
105 |   worker.once("exit", () => {
106 |     if (gitWorker === worker) gitWorker = null;
107 |   });

109 | }

  1 | import { ipcMain } from "electron";
  2 | import type { UtilityProcess } from "electron";
  3 | import { execFile } from "node:child_process";
  4 | import { promisify } from "node:util";
  5 | import os from "node:os";
  6 | import * as storeLib from "./lib/store";
  7 | import { callGranite, aiConfigStatus, configuredModel } from "./lib/granite";
  8 | import { startOAuthFlow, fetchProfile } from "./oauth-server";
  9 | import * as github from "./lib/github";
 10 | import * as gitlab from "./lib/gitlab";
 11 | import { getProviderRateLimitSnapshots } from "./lib/provider-http";
 12 | 
 13 | const execFileAsync = promisify(execFile);
 14 | 
 15 | /**
 16 |  * Resolve a friendly name for the local user when no remote auth is connected.
 17 |  * Tries `git config --global user.name` first (typically the developer's full
 18 |  * name), then `git config --global user.email` local-part, then the OS username
 19 |  * as a last resort. Returns `null` only if all three lookups fail.
 20 |  */
 21 | async function readLocalIdentity(): Promise<{ name: string | null }> {
 22 |   // 1. Try git global user.name. Most developers have this set to their name.
 23 |   try {
 24 |     const { stdout } = await execFileAsync("git", [
 25 |       "config",
 26 |       "--global",
 27 |       "user.name",
 28 |     ]);
 29 |     const name = stdout.trim();
 30 |     if (name) return { name };
 31 |   } catch {
 32 |     // Git not installed or no global user.name — fall through.
 33 |   }
 34 | 
 35 |   // 2. Try the local-part of git global user.email.
 36 |   try {
 37 |     const { stdout } = await execFileAsync("git", [
 38 |       "config",
 39 |       "--global",
 40 |       "user.email",
 41 |     ]);
 42 |     const email = stdout.trim();
 43 |     if (email.includes("@")) {
 44 |       const localPart = email.split("@")[0];
 45 |       if (localPart) return { name: localPart };
 46 |     }
 47 |   } catch {
 48 |     // No email configured — fall through.
 49 |   }
 50 | 
 51 |   // 3. OS username as a final fallback.
 52 |   try {
 53 |     const info = os.userInfo();
 54 |     if (info.username) return { name: info.username };
 55 |   } catch {
 56 |     // Some sandboxes block userInfo — return null.
 57 |   }
 58 | 
 59 |   return { name: null };
 60 | }

 65 |   error?: string;

 75 |   value: T;

 82 |   | "git:scan"

 96 | function asWorkerReply(message: unknown): WorkerReply | null {
 97 |   if (!message || typeof message !== "object") return null;
 98 |   const reply = message as Partial<WorkerReply>;
 99 |   return typeof reply.id === "string" ? (reply as WorkerReply) : null;
100 | }
101 | 
102 | function unwrapMessageData(message: unknown): unknown {
103 |   if (message && typeof message === "object" && "data" in message) {
104 |     return (message as { data: unknown }).data;
105 |   }
106 |   return message;
107 | }
108 | 
109 | function asWorkerEvent(message: unknown): WorkerEvent | null {
110 |   if (!message || typeof message !== "object") return null;
111 |   const event = message as Partial<WorkerEvent>;
112 |   return typeof event.event === "string" ? (event as WorkerEvent) : null;
113 | }
114 | 
115 | function readPRDetailOption(value: unknown): number | null {
116 |   if (!value || typeof value !== "object" || Array.isArray(value)) return null;
117 |   const opts = value as { mode?: unknown; number?: unknown };
118 |   if (opts.mode !== "detail") return null;
119 |   return typeof opts.number === "number" && Number.isInteger(opts.number) && opts.number > 0
120 |     ? opts.number
121 |     : null;
122 | }
123 | 
124 | function readForceOption(value: unknown): boolean {
125 |   if (!value || typeof value !== "object" || Array.isArray(value)) return false;
126 |   return (value as { force?: unknown }).force === true;
127 | }
128 | 
129 | function readMRDetailOption(value: unknown): number | null {
130 |   if (!value || typeof value !== "object" || Array.isArray(value)) return null;
131 |   const opts = value as { mode?: unknown; iid?: unknown };
132 |   if (opts.mode !== "detail") return null;
133 |   return typeof opts.iid === "number" && Number.isInteger(opts.iid) && opts.iid > 0
134 |     ? opts.iid
135 |     : null;
136 | }
137 | 
138 | function readIssueDetailOption(value: unknown): number | null {
139 |   if (!value || typeof value !== "object" || Array.isArray(value)) return null;
140 |   const opts = value as { mode?: unknown; number?: unknown };
141 |   if (opts.mode !== "detail") return null;
142 |   return typeof opts.number === "number" && Number.isInteger(opts.number) && opts.number > 0
143 |     ? opts.number
144 |     : null;
145 | }

147 | function assertProvider(value: unknown): Provider {
148 |   if (value === "github" || value === "gitlab") return value;
149 |   throw new Error("Provider must be 'github' or 'gitlab'.");
150 | }
151 | 
152 | function assertPositiveInteger(value: unknown, name: string): number {
153 |   if (typeof value === "number" && Number.isInteger(value) && value > 0) return value;
154 |   throw new Error(`${name} must be a positive integer.`);
155 | }
156 | 
157 | function assertBoundedCommentBody(value: unknown): string {
158 |   if (typeof value !== "string") {
159 |     throw new Error("Comment body must be a string.");
160 |   }
161 |   const body = value.trim();
162 |   if (!body) throw new Error("Comment body cannot be empty.");
163 |   if (body.length > 20_000) {
164 |     throw new Error("Comment body is too large.");
165 |   }
166 |   return body;
167 | }
168 | 
169 | function assertStoreKey(value: unknown): string {
170 |   if (typeof value !== "string" || !/^[A-Za-z0-9:_-]{1,80}$/.test(value)) {
171 |     throw new Error("Store key contains unsupported characters.");
172 |   }
173 |   return value;
174 | }
175 | 
176 | function assertGitLabProjectId(value: unknown): string {
177 |   if (typeof value !== "string" || !value.trim() || value.length > 300) {
178 |     throw new Error("GitLab project id must be a non-empty string.");
179 |   }
180 |   if (/[\0\r\n]/.test(value)) {
181 |     throw new Error("GitLab project id contains unsupported characters.");
182 |   }
183 |   return value;
184 | }
185 | 
186 | function recordGitWorkerChange(event: WorkerEvent): void {
187 |   if (event.event !== "git:changed" || !event.repoPath) return;
188 |   const timestamp = typeof event.timestamp === "number" ? event.timestamp : Date.now();
189 |   const repositories = storeLib.getStoreValue("repositories");
190 |   if (!Array.isArray(repositories)) return;
191 | 
192 |   const nextRepositories = repositories.map((repo) => {
193 |     if (
194 |       repo &&
195 |       typeof repo === "object" &&
196 |       (repo as Partial<storeLib.Repository>).local_path === event.repoPath
197 |     ) {
198 |       return { ...repo, last_synced: timestamp };
199 |     }
200 |     return repo;
201 |   }) as storeLib.Repository[];
202 | 
203 |   const changedRepo = nextRepositories.find(
204 |     (repo) => repo.local_path === event.repoPath,
205 |   );
206 |   storeLib.setStoreValue("repositories", nextRepositories);
207 |   if (!changedRepo) return;
208 | 
209 |   const activity = storeLib.getStoreValue("activity");
210 |   const existing = Array.isArray(activity)
211 |     ? (activity as storeLib.ActivityItem[])
212 |     : [];
213 |   const id = `fs-change:${changedRepo.id}`;
214 |   const nextActivity: storeLib.ActivityItem[] = [
215 |     {
216 |       id,
217 |       repo_id: changedRepo.id,
218 |       type: "fs_change",
219 |       title: "Workspace files changed",
220 |       metadata: { path: event.repoPath },
221 |       timestamp,
222 |     },
223 |     ...existing.filter((item) => item.id !== id),
224 |   ].slice(0, 500);
225 |   storeLib.setStoreValue("activity", nextActivity);
226 | }

228 | const REMOTE_DATA_CACHE_KEY = "remote_data_cache";
229 | const AI_AUDIT_LOG_KEY = "ai_audit_log";
230 | const REMOTE_LIST_TTL_MS = 2 * 60 * 1000;
231 | const REMOTE_DETAIL_TTL_MS = 5 * 60 * 1000;
232 | const MAX_REMOTE_CACHE_ENTRIES = 200;
233 | const MAX_AI_AUDIT_ENTRIES = 120;
234 | const revalidatingRemoteKeys = new Set<string>();

236 | function remoteCache(): Record<string, unknown> {
237 |   const cache = storeLib.getStoreValue(REMOTE_DATA_CACHE_KEY);
238 |   if (!cache || typeof cache !== "object" || Array.isArray(cache)) return {};
239 |   return cache as Record<string, unknown>;
240 | }
241 | 
242 | async function withRemoteCache<T>(
243 |   key: string,
244 |   ttlMs: number,
245 |   force: boolean,
246 |   fetchFresh: () => Promise<T>,
247 | ): Promise<T> {
248 |   const cache = remoteCache();
249 |   const cached = cache[key] as Partial<RemoteCacheEntry<T>> | undefined;
250 |   if (
251 |     !force &&
252 |     cached &&
253 |     typeof cached.timestamp === "number" &&
254 |     "value" in cached
255 |   ) {
256 |     if (Date.now() - cached.timestamp >= ttlMs) {
257 |       revalidateRemoteCache(key, fetchFresh);
258 |     }
259 |     return cached.value as T;
260 |   }
261 | 
262 |   const value = await fetchFresh();
263 |   storeLib.setStoreValue(REMOTE_DATA_CACHE_KEY, pruneRemoteCache({
264 |     ...cache,
265 |     [key]: { value, timestamp: Date.now() },
266 |   }));
267 |   return value;
268 | }
269 | 
270 | function revalidateRemoteCache<T>(
271 |   key: string,
272 |   fetchFresh: () => Promise<T>,
273 | ): void {
274 |   if (revalidatingRemoteKeys.has(key)) return;
275 |   revalidatingRemoteKeys.add(key);
276 |   void fetchFresh()
277 |     .then((value) => {
278 |       const cache = remoteCache();
279 |       storeLib.setStoreValue(REMOTE_DATA_CACHE_KEY, pruneRemoteCache({
280 |         ...cache,
281 |         [key]: { value, timestamp: Date.now() },
282 |       }));
283 |     })
284 |     .catch(() => {
285 |       // Stale cache remains usable; transient provider failures are surfaced on forced refresh.
286 |     })
287 |     .finally(() => {
288 |       revalidatingRemoteKeys.delete(key);
289 |     });
290 | }
291 | 
292 | function pruneRemoteCache(cache: Record<string, unknown>): Record<string, unknown> {
293 |   const now = Date.now();
294 |   const entries = Object.entries(cache)
295 |     .filter(([, entry]) => {
296 |       if (!entry || typeof entry !== "object" || Array.isArray(entry)) return false;
297 |       const timestamp = (entry as Partial<RemoteCacheEntry<unknown>>).timestamp;
298 |       return typeof timestamp === "number" && now - timestamp <= REMOTE_DETAIL_TTL_MS * 4;
299 |     })
300 |     .sort((a, b) => {
301 |       const aTimestamp = ((a[1] as Partial<RemoteCacheEntry<unknown>>).timestamp ?? 0);
302 |       const bTimestamp = ((b[1] as Partial<RemoteCacheEntry<unknown>>).timestamp ?? 0);
303 |       return bTimestamp - aTimestamp;
304 |     })
305 |     .slice(0, MAX_REMOTE_CACHE_ENTRIES);
306 |   return Object.fromEntries(entries);
307 | }
308 | 
309 | function recordAIAudit(entry: {
310 |   feature: string;
311 |   model: string;
312 |   status: "ok" | "error";
313 |   promptChars: number;
314 |   responseChars: number;
315 |   durationMs: number;
316 |   error?: string;
317 | }): void {
318 |   const existing = storeLib.getStoreValue(AI_AUDIT_LOG_KEY);
319 |   const audit = Array.isArray(existing) ? existing : [];
320 |   storeLib.setStoreValue(AI_AUDIT_LOG_KEY, [
321 |     {
322 |       id: `ai:${Date.now()}:${Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 8)}`,
323 |       timestamp: Date.now(),
324 |       ...entry,
325 |     },
326 |     ...audit,
327 |   ].slice(0, MAX_AI_AUDIT_ENTRIES));
328 | }
329 | 
330 | function inferAIFeature(systemPrompt: string): string {
331 |   const prompt = systemPrompt.toLowerCase();
332 |   if (prompt.includes("daily standup")) return "standup";
333 |   if (prompt.includes("single pull request file patch")) return "pr_file_change";
334 |   if (prompt.includes("diff hunks")) return "pr_hunk_review";
335 |   if (prompt.includes("pull request")) return "pr_review";
336 |   if (prompt.includes("github issue")) return "issue_triage";
337 |   if (prompt.includes("worktree")) return "worktree_compare";
338 |   if (prompt.includes("repository onboarding") || prompt.includes("repo brief")) return "repo_brief";
339 |   if (prompt.includes("conventional commit")) return "commit_assistant";
340 |   if (prompt.includes("code diff")) return "impact_analysis";
341 |   if (prompt.includes("code or diff selection")) return "code_explain";
342 |   if (prompt.includes("stash")) return "stash_annotator";
343 |   if (prompt.includes("repair")) return "json_repair";
344 |   return "granite";
345 | }
346 | 
347 | export function registerIPCHandlers(gitWorker: UtilityProcess) {
348 |   let nextGitMessageId = 0;
349 |   const pendingGitMessages = new Map<
350 |     string,
351 |     { resolve: (value: unknown) => void; reject: (error: Error) => void }
352 |   >();
353 | 
354 |   gitWorker.on("message", (message) => {
355 |     const payload = unwrapMessageData(message);
356 |     const reply = asWorkerReply(payload);
357 |     if (!reply) {
358 |       const event = asWorkerEvent(payload);
359 |       if (event) recordGitWorkerChange(event);
360 |       return;
361 |     }
362 |     const pending = pendingGitMessages.get(reply.id);
363 |     if (!pending) return;
364 |     pendingGitMessages.delete(reply.id);
365 |     if (reply.error) {
366 |       pending.reject(new Error(reply.error));
367 |       return;
368 |     }
369 |     pending.resolve(reply.result);
370 |   });
371 | 
372 |   gitWorker.once("exit", () => {
373 |     for (const pending of pendingGitMessages.values()) {
374 |       pending.reject(new Error("Git worker exited before completing the request."));
375 |     }
376 |     pendingGitMessages.clear();
377 |   });
378 | 
379 |   function invokeGit<T>(channel: GitChannel, args: unknown[]): Promise<T> {
380 |     const id = `git-${nextGitMessageId++}`;
381 |     return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
382 |       pendingGitMessages.set(id, {
383 |         resolve: (value) => resolve(value as T),
384 |         reject,
385 |       });
386 |       gitWorker.postMessage({ id, channel, args });
387 |     });
388 |   }

390 |   // AUTH CHANNELS (3)
391 |   // ============================================================

393 |   ipcMain.handle("auth:connect", async (_, provider: unknown) => {
394 |     const safeProvider = assertProvider(provider);
395 |     const token = await startOAuthFlow(safeProvider);
396 |     const profile = await fetchProfile(safeProvider, token);
397 |     storeLib.setAccount(safeProvider, {
398 |       username: profile.username,
399 |       token,
400 |       avatar_url: profile.avatar_url,
401 |     });
402 |     // Token stays main-process only. Renderer gets non-sensitive profile data.
403 |     return { username: profile.username, avatar_url: profile.avatar_url };
404 |   });
405 |

407 |     "auth:disconnect",

417 |       github: !!githubAccount,
418 |       gitlab: !!gitlabAccount,

424 |             }

429 |               avatar_url: gitlabAccount.avatar_url,
430 |             }
431 |           : null,

504 |   function githubToken(): string {
505 |     const acct = storeLib.getAccount("github");
506 |     if (!acct?.token) throw new Error("GitHub not connected. Use auth:connect first.");
507 |     return acct.token;
508 |   }
509 | 
510 |   ipcMain.handle("github:repos", async () =>
511 |     withRemoteCache(
512 |       "github:repos",
513 |       REMOTE_LIST_TTL_MS,
514 |       false,
515 |       () => github.listRepos(githubToken()),
516 |     ),
517 |   );
518 | 
519 |   ipcMain.handle(
520 |     "github:issues",
521 |     async (_, repoFullName?: string, options?: unknown) => {
522 |       const selectedRepo = typeof repoFullName === "string" ? repoFullName.trim() : "";
523 |       const token = githubToken();
524 |       const detail = readIssueDetailOption(options);
525 |       const force = readForceOption(options);
526 |       if (detail !== null) {
527 |         const { owner, repo } = github.parseFullName(selectedRepo);
528 |         return withRemoteCache(
529 |           `github:issue-detail:${selectedRepo}:${detail}`,
530 |           REMOTE_DETAIL_TTL_MS,
531 |           force,
532 |           () => github.fetchIssueDetail(token, owner, repo, detail),
533 |         );
534 |       }
535 |       if (!selectedRepo) {
536 |         return withRemoteCache(
537 |           "github:issues:all",
538 |           REMOTE_LIST_TTL_MS,
539 |           force,
540 |           () => github.listUserIssues(token),
541 |         );
542 |       }
543 |       const { owner, repo } = github.parseFullName(selectedRepo);
544 |       return withRemoteCache(
545 |         `github:issues:${selectedRepo}`,
546 |         REMOTE_LIST_TTL_MS,
547 |         force,
548 |         () => github.listIssues(token, owner, repo),
549 |       );
550 |     },
551 |   );
552 | 
553 |   ipcMain.handle(
554 |     "github:prs",
555 |     async (_, repoFullName: string, options?: unknown) => {
556 |       const { owner, repo } = github.parseFullName(repoFullName);
557 |       const token = githubToken();
558 |       const detail = readPRDetailOption(options);
559 |       const force = readForceOption(options);
560 |       if (detail !== null) {

563 |           REMOTE_DETAIL_TTL_MS,
564 |           force,
565 |           () => github.fetchPRDetail(token, owner, repo, detail),
566 |         );
567 |       }
568 |       return withRemoteCache(
569 |         `github:prs:${repoFullName}`,
570 |         REMOTE_LIST_TTL_MS,
571 |         force,
572 |         () => github.listPRs(token, owner, repo),
573 |       );
574 |     },
575 |   );

644 |   // GitLab issues mirror the GitHub channel: a single handler that returns
645 |   // either a list or a detail payload depending on the `mode` option. The
646 |   // detail payload conforms to GitHubIssueDetail so the UI layer doesn't
647 |   // need provider-specific branching.
648 |   ipcMain.handle(
649 |     "gitlab:issues",
650 |     async (_, projectId: string, options?: unknown) => {
651 |       const safeProjectId = assertGitLabProjectId(projectId);
652 |       const token = gitlabToken();
653 |       const detail = readIssueDetailOption(options);
654 |       const force = readForceOption(options);
655 |       if (detail !== null) {
656 |         return withRemoteCache(
657 |           `gitlab:issue-detail:${safeProjectId}:${detail}`,
658 |           REMOTE_DETAIL_TTL_MS,
659 |           force,
660 |           () => gitlab.fetchGitLabIssueDetail(token, safeProjectId, detail),
661 |         );
662 |       }
663 |       return withRemoteCache(
664 |         `gitlab:issues:${safeProjectId}`,
665 |         REMOTE_LIST_TTL_MS,
666 |         force,
667 |         () => gitlab.listGitLabIssues(token, safeProjectId),
668 |       );
669 |     },
670 |   );

674 |     return withRemoteCache(

676 |       REMOTE_LIST_TTL_MS,
677 |       false,
678 |       () => gitlab.listPipelines(gitlabToken(), safeProjectId),
679 |     );
680 |   });

694 |   // ============================================================
695 |   // AI CHANNELS (2)
696 |   // ============================================================
697 | 
698 |   ipcMain.handle(
699 |     "ai:complete",
700 |     async (_, systemPrompt: string, userPrompt: string) => {
701 |       const started = Date.now();
702 |       const promptChars = systemPrompt.length + userPrompt.length;
703 |       const feature = inferAIFeature(systemPrompt);
704 |       const model = configuredModel();
705 |       try {
706 |         const response = await callGranite(systemPrompt, userPrompt);
707 |         recordAIAudit({
708 |           feature,
709 |           model,
710 |           status: "ok",
711 |           promptChars,
712 |           responseChars: response.length,
713 |           durationMs: Date.now() - started,
714 |         });
715 |         return response;
716 |       } catch (error) {
717 |         recordAIAudit({
718 |           feature,
719 |           model,
720 |           status: "error",
721 |           promptChars,
722 |           responseChars: 0,
723 |           durationMs: Date.now() - started,
724 |           error: error instanceof Error ? error.message.slice(0, 180) : "AI request failed",
725 |         });
726 |         throw error;
727 |       }
728 |     },
729 |   );
730 | 
731 |   ipcMain.handle("ai:status", () => aiConfigStatus());
732 | 
733 |   // ============================================================
734 |   // STORE CHANNELS (3)
735 |   // ============================================================
736 |   // 'accounts' holds OAuth tokens — must never traverse the renderer boundary.
737 |   const FORBIDDEN_KEYS = new Set(["accounts"]);
738 |   // Fields inside 'settings' that hold secrets — stripped on the way out.
739 |   const SETTINGS_SECRETS = new Set(["watsonx_api_key", "watsonx_project_id"]);
740 | 
741 |   function sanitize(key: string, value: unknown): unknown {
742 |     if (key === "settings" && value && typeof value === "object") {
743 |       const out: Record<string, unknown> = {};
744 |       for (const [k, v] of Object.entries(value)) {
745 |         if (!SETTINGS_SECRETS.has(k)) out[k] = v;
746 |       }
747 |       return out;
748 |     }
749 |     return value;
750 |   }
751 | 
752 |   ipcMain.handle("store:get", async (_, rawKey: unknown) => {
753 |     const key = assertStoreKey(rawKey);
754 |     if (FORBIDDEN_KEYS.has(key)) {
755 |       throw new Error(`Access to '${key}' is restricted to the main process.`);
756 |     }
757 |     return sanitize(key, storeLib.getStoreValue(key));
758 |   });
759 | 
760 |   ipcMain.handle("store:set", async (_, rawKey: unknown, value: unknown) => {
761 |     const key = assertStoreKey(rawKey);
762 |     if (FORBIDDEN_KEYS.has(key)) {
763 |       throw new Error(`Access to '${key}' is restricted to the main process.`);
764 |     }
765 |     if (key === "settings" && value && typeof value === "object") {
766 |       // Renderer cannot write secret settings fields. Preserve any existing secret values
767 |       // so a partial settings write from the renderer doesn't wipe them.
768 |       const existing = (storeLib.getStoreValue("settings") as Record<string, unknown>) ?? {};
769 |       const merged: Record<string, unknown> = { ...value };
770 |       for (const secret of SETTINGS_SECRETS) {
771 |         if (existing[secret] !== undefined) merged[secret] = existing[secret];
772 |         else delete merged[secret];
773 |       }
774 |       storeLib.setStoreValue(key, merged);
775 |       return;
776 |     }
777 |     storeLib.setStoreValue(key, value);
778 |   });
779 | 
780 |   ipcMain.handle("store:list", async () => {
781 |     return storeLib.listStoreKeys().filter((k) => !FORBIDDEN_KEYS.has(k));
782 |   });
783 | }

81 |   ai: {

83 |       ipcRenderer.invoke("ai:complete", systemPrompt, userPrompt),
84 |     status: () => ipcRenderer.invoke("ai:status"),
85 |   },
86 | 
87 |   store: {
88 |     get: (key: string) => ipcRenderer.invoke("store:get", key),
89 |     set: (key: string, value: unknown) =>
90 |       ipcRenderer.invoke("store:set", key, value),
91 |     list: () => ipcRenderer.invoke("store:list"),
92 |   },
93 | };
94 | 
95 | contextBridge.exposeInMainWorld("api", api);
96 | 
97 | export type API = typeof api;
</content>

  1 | import { Component, useEffect, type ErrorInfo, type ReactNode } from "react";
  2 | import { Dashboard } from "./screens/Dashboard";
  3 | import { RepoDetail } from "./screens/RepoDetail";
  4 | import { PullRequests } from "./screens/PullRequests";
  5 | import { PRDetail } from "./screens/PRDetail";
  6 | import { GitHubIssues } from "./screens/GitHubIssues";
  7 | import { GitHubIssueDetail } from "./screens/GitHubIssueDetail";
  8 | import { Repositories } from "./screens/Repositories";
  9 | import { SettingsScreen } from "./screens/Settings";
 10 | import { AIPanel } from "./components/ai/AIPanel";
 11 | import { CommandPalette } from "./components/CommandPalette";
 12 | import { LocalChangesPanel } from "./components/LocalChangesPanel";
 13 | import { RouteFrame } from "./components/RouteFrame";
 14 | import { useNav, type Screen } from "./store/useNav";
 15 | import { useCommandPalette } from "./store/useCommandPalette";
 16 | import { useAIPanel } from "./store/useAIPanel";
 17 | import { useTheme } from "./store/useTheme";
 18 | import "./App.css";
 19 | 
 20 | interface RouteErrorBoundaryProps {
 21 |   screen: Screen;
 22 |   onReset: () => void;
 23 |   children: ReactNode;
 24 | }
 25 | 
 26 | interface RouteErrorBoundaryState {
 27 |   error: Error | null;
 28 | }
 29 | 
 30 | class RouteErrorBoundary extends Component<
 31 |   RouteErrorBoundaryProps,
 32 |   RouteErrorBoundaryState
 33 | > {
 34 |   state: RouteErrorBoundaryState = { error: null };
 35 | 
 36 |   static getDerivedStateFromError(error: Error): RouteErrorBoundaryState {
 37 |     return { error };
 38 |   }
 39 | 
 40 |   componentDidCatch(error: Error, info: ErrorInfo) {
 41 |     console.error("[overcode-route-error]", error, info.componentStack);
 42 |   }
 43 | 
 44 |   componentDidUpdate(prevProps: RouteErrorBoundaryProps) {
 45 |     if (prevProps.screen !== this.props.screen && this.state.error) {
 46 |       this.setState({ error: null });
 47 |     }
 48 |   }
 49 | 
 50 |   render() {
 51 |     if (!this.state.error) return this.props.children;
 52 |     return (
 53 |       <main className="route-error">
 54 |         <span className="route-error-kicker">Renderer recovered</span>
 55 |         <h1>Could not render this view</h1>
 56 |         <p>{this.state.error.message || "Unexpected renderer error."}</p>
 57 |         <button type="button" onClick={this.props.onReset}>
 58 |           Back to dashboard
 59 |         </button>
 60 |       </main>
 61 |     );
 62 |   }
 63 | }
 64 | 
 65 | function renderScreen(screen: ReturnType<typeof useNav.getState>["screen"]) {
 66 |   if (screen === "repo-detail") return <RepoDetail />;
 67 |   if (screen === "prs") return <PullRequests />;
 68 |   if (screen === "pr-detail") return <PRDetail />;
 69 |   if (screen === "issues") return <GitHubIssues />;
 70 |   if (screen === "issue-detail") return <GitHubIssueDetail />;
 71 |   if (screen === "repositories") return <Repositories />;
 72 |   if (screen === "settings") return <SettingsScreen />;
 73 |   return <Dashboard />;
 74 | }
 75 | 
 76 | const NUM_TO_SCREEN: Record<string, Screen> = {
 77 |   "1": "dashboard",
 78 |   "2": "repositories",
 79 |   "3": "prs",
 80 |   "5": "issues",
 81 | };
 82 | 
 83 | function App() {
 84 |   const screen = useNav((s) => s.screen);
 85 |   const navigate = useNav((s) => s.navigate);
 86 |   const toggleCmd = useCommandPalette((s) => s.toggle);
 87 |   const toggleAI = useAIPanel((s) => s.toggle);
 88 |   const toggleTheme = useTheme((s) => s.toggle);
 89 | 
 90 |   useEffect(() => {
 91 |     function onKey(e: KeyboardEvent) {
 92 |       const meta = e.metaKey || e.ctrlKey;
 93 |       if (!meta) return;
 94 |       const key = e.key.toLowerCase();
 95 |       if (key === "k" && !e.shiftKey) {
 96 |         e.preventDefault();
 97 |         toggleCmd();
 98 |         return;
 99 |       }
100 |       if (key === "j" && e.shiftKey) {
101 |         e.preventDefault();
102 |         toggleTheme();
103 |         return;
104 |       }
105 |       if (e.key === "4") {
106 |         e.preventDefault();
107 |         toggleAI();
108 |         return;
109 |       }
110 |       const target = NUM_TO_SCREEN[e.key];
111 |       if (target) {
112 |         e.preventDefault();
113 |         navigate(target);
114 |       }
115 |     }
116 |     window.addEventListener("keydown", onKey);
117 |     return () => window.removeEventListener("keydown", onKey);
118 |   }, [toggleCmd, toggleAI, toggleTheme, navigate]);
119 | 
120 |   return (
121 |     <>
122 |       {/* App shell: the rounded paper window the screens live inside.
123 |           Overlays (AIPanel, CommandPalette) stay outside so they can use
124 |           position: fixed against the viewport. */}
125 |       <div className="app-shell">
126 |         <RouteErrorBoundary screen={screen} onReset={() => navigate("dashboard")}>
127 |           <RouteFrame screen={screen}>{renderScreen(screen)}</RouteFrame>
128 |         </RouteErrorBoundary>
129 |       </div>
130 |       <AIPanel />
131 |       <CommandPalette />
132 |       <LocalChangesPanel />
133 |     </>
134 |   );
135 | }
136 | 
137 | export default App;
</content>

<content lines="1-320">
  1 | // Git Worker - Utility Process
  2 | // Handles all git operations via simple-git to prevent UI freezing
  3 | 
  4 | import chokidar, { type FSWatcher } from "chokidar";
  5 | import * as gitOps from "../lib/git-ops";
  6 | 
  7 | const gitChannels = [
  8 |   "git:scan",
  9 |   "git:status",
 10 |   "git:log",
 11 |   "git:stashes",
 12 |   "git:stash-show",
 13 |   "git:worktrees",
 14 |   "git:file",
 15 |   "git:divergence",
 16 |   "git:push",
 17 |   "git:pull",
 18 |   "git:commit",
 19 |   "git:stash-pop",
 20 |   "git:stash-drop",
 21 | ] as const;
 22 | 
 23 | type GitChannel = (typeof gitChannels)[number];
 24 | 
 25 | interface WorkerMessage {
 26 |   id: string;
 27 |   channel: string;
 28 |   args: unknown[];
 29 | }
 30 | 
 31 | interface WatchedRepository {
 32 |   local_path: string;
 33 | }
 34 | 
 35 | const watchDebounceMs = 500;
 36 | const watchersByRepoPath = new Map<string, FSWatcher>();
 37 | const pendingChangeTimers = new Map<string, NodeJS.Timeout>();
 38 | 
 39 | function isGitChannel(channel: string): channel is GitChannel {
 40 |   return (gitChannels as readonly string[]).includes(channel);
 41 | }
 42 | 
 43 | function isWorkerMessage(message: unknown): message is WorkerMessage {
 44 |   if (!message || typeof message !== "object") return false;
 45 |   const candidate = message as Record<string, unknown>;
 46 |   return (
 47 |     typeof candidate.id === "string" &&
 48 |     typeof candidate.channel === "string" &&
 49 |     Array.isArray(candidate.args)
 50 |   );
 51 | }
 52 | 
 53 | function unwrapMessageData(message: unknown): unknown {
 54 |   if (message && typeof message === "object" && "data" in message) {
 55 |     return (message as { data: unknown }).data;
 56 |   }
 57 |   return message;
 58 | }
 59 | 
 60 | function requireString(args: unknown[], index: number, name: string): string {
 61 |   const value = args[index];
 62 |   if (typeof value !== "string") {
 63 |     throw new Error(`${name} must be a string`);
 64 |   }
 65 |   return value;
 66 | }
 67 | 
 68 | function requireStringArray(args: unknown[], index: number, name: string): string[] {
 69 |   const value = args[index];
 70 |   if (!Array.isArray(value) || !value.every((item) => typeof item === "string")) {
 71 |     throw new Error(`${name} must be an array of strings`);
 72 |   }
 73 |   return value;
 74 | }
 75 | 
 76 | function optionalNumber(args: unknown[], index: number, name: string): number | undefined {
 77 |   const value = args[index];
 78 |   if (value === undefined) return undefined;
 79 |   if (typeof value !== "number" || !Number.isFinite(value)) {
 80 |     throw new Error(`${name} must be a number`);
 81 |   }
 82 |   return value;
 83 | }
 84 | 
 85 | function optionalPositiveInteger(
 86 |   args: unknown[],
 87 |   index: number,
 88 |   name: string,
 89 |   max: number,
 90 | ): number | undefined {
 91 |   const value = optionalNumber(args, index, name);
 92 |   if (value === undefined) return undefined;
 93 |   if (!Number.isInteger(value) || value < 1) {
 94 |     throw new Error(`${name} must be a positive integer`);
 95 |   }
 96 |   return Math.min(value, max);
 97 | }
 98 | 
 99 | function readScanMode(value: unknown): "list" | "candidates" {
100 |   if (value && typeof value === "object" && !Array.isArray(value)) {
101 |     const mode = (value as { mode?: unknown }).mode;
102 |     if (mode === "candidates") return "candidates";
103 |   }
104 |   return "list";
105 | }
106 | 
107 | function readWorktreeOptions(value: unknown): gitOps.WorktreeOptions {
108 |   if (!value || typeof value !== "object" || Array.isArray(value)) return undefined;
109 |   const options = value as { mode?: unknown; targetPath?: unknown; base?: unknown };
110 |   if (options.mode === "summary-input") {
111 |     return {
112 |       mode: "summary-input",
113 |       targetPath: typeof options.targetPath === "string" ? options.targetPath : undefined,
114 |       base: typeof options.base === "string" ? options.base : undefined,
115 |     };
116 |   }
117 |   return { mode: "list" };
118 | }
119 | 
120 | function readFileOptions(value: unknown): gitOps.RepoFileReadOptions {
121 |   if (!value || typeof value !== "object" || Array.isArray(value)) return {};
122 |   const options = value as { ref?: unknown; maxBytes?: unknown };
123 |   return {
124 |     ref: typeof options.ref === "string" ? options.ref : undefined,
125 |     maxBytes: typeof options.maxBytes === "number" ? options.maxBytes : undefined,
126 |   };
127 | }
128 | 
129 | function readStatusOptions(value: unknown): gitOps.GitStatusOptions {
130 |   if (!value || typeof value !== "object" || Array.isArray(value)) return {};
131 |   const mode = (value as { mode?: unknown }).mode;
132 |   if (mode === "lite" || mode === "diff" || mode === "health" || mode === "full") {
133 |     return { mode };
134 |   }
135 |   return {};
136 | }
137 | 
138 | function optionalString(args: unknown[], index: number, name: string): string | undefined {
139 |   const value = args[index];
140 |   if (value === undefined) return undefined;
141 |   if (typeof value !== "string") {
142 |     throw new Error(`${name} must be a string`);
143 |   }
144 |   return value;
145 | }
146 | 
147 | function isWatchedRepository(value: unknown): value is WatchedRepository {
148 |   return (
149 |     Boolean(value) &&
150 |     typeof value === "object" &&
151 |     typeof (value as Partial<WatchedRepository>).local_path === "string"
152 |   );
153 | }
154 | 
155 | function shouldIgnoreWatchPath(pathToCheck: string): boolean {
156 |   return /(^|[/\\])(\.git|node_modules|bower_components|jspm_packages|dist|dist-electron|build|out|coverage|target|vendor|third_party|\.next|\.nuxt|\.output|\.cache|\.turbo|\.pnpm|\.yarn|\.npm|\.venv|venv|env)([/\\]|$)/.test(
157 |     pathToCheck,
158 |   );
159 | }
160 | 
161 | function emitRepoChange(repoPath: string): void {
162 |   const pending = pendingChangeTimers.get(repoPath);
163 |   if (pending) clearTimeout(pending);
164 |   pendingChangeTimers.set(
165 |     repoPath,
166 |     setTimeout(() => {
167 |       pendingChangeTimers.delete(repoPath);
168 |       process.parentPort?.postMessage({
169 |         event: "git:changed",
170 |         repoPath,
171 |         timestamp: Date.now(),
172 |       });
173 |     }, watchDebounceMs),
174 |   );
175 | }
176 | 
177 | function watchRepositories(repositories: unknown): void {
178 |   if (!Array.isArray(repositories)) return;
179 |   for (const repository of repositories) {
180 |     if (!isWatchedRepository(repository)) continue;
181 |     const repoPath = repository.local_path;
182 |     if (watchersByRepoPath.has(repoPath)) continue;
183 |     const watcher = chokidar.watch(repoPath, {
184 |       ignored: shouldIgnoreWatchPath,
185 |       ignoreInitial: true,
186 |       awaitWriteFinish: {
187 |         stabilityThreshold: 500,
188 |         pollInterval: 100,
189 |       },
190 |     });
191 |     watcher.on("all", () => emitRepoChange(repoPath));
192 |     watcher.on("error", () => {
193 |       void watcher.close();
194 |       watchersByRepoPath.delete(repoPath);
195 |     });
196 |     watchersByRepoPath.set(repoPath, watcher);
197 |   }
198 | }
199 | 
200 | async function handleGitMessage({ channel, args }: WorkerMessage): Promise<unknown> {
201 |   if (!isGitChannel(channel)) {
202 |     throw new Error(`Unknown channel: ${channel}`);
203 |   }
204 | 
205 |   switch (channel) {
206 |     case "git:scan":
207 |       {
208 |         const directories = requireStringArray(args, 0, "directories");
209 |         const mode = readScanMode(args[1]);
210 |         if (mode === "candidates") {
211 |           return gitOps.scanWorkspaceCandidates(directories);
212 |         }
213 |         const repositories = await gitOps.scanRepos(directories);
214 |         watchRepositories(repositories);
215 |         return repositories;
216 |       }
217 | 
218 |     case "git:status":
219 |       return gitOps.getStatus(
220 |         requireString(args, 0, "repoPath"),
221 |         readStatusOptions(args[1]),
222 |       );
223 | 
224 |     case "git:log":
225 |       {
226 |         const repoPath = requireString(args, 0, "repoPath");
227 |         const hash = optionalString(args, 2, "hash");
228 |         const opts = args[3];
229 |         if (hash && opts && typeof opts === "object" && !Array.isArray(opts) && (opts as { mode?: unknown }).mode === "stat") {
230 |           return gitOps.getCommitStat(repoPath, hash);
231 |         }
232 |         if (hash) return gitOps.showCommit(repoPath, hash);
233 |         return gitOps.getLog(repoPath, optionalPositiveInteger(args, 1, "maxCount", 500));
234 |       }
235 | 
236 |     case "git:stashes":
237 |       return gitOps.getStashes(requireString(args, 0, "repoPath"));
238 | 
239 |     case "git:stash-show":
240 |       return gitOps.getStashShow(
241 |         requireString(args, 0, "repoPath"),
242 |         requireString(args, 1, "stashRef"),
243 |       );
244 | 
245 |     case "git:worktrees":
246 |       return gitOps.getWorktrees(
247 |         requireString(args, 0, "repoPath"),
248 |         readWorktreeOptions(args[1]),
249 |       );
250 | 
251 |     case "git:file":
252 |       return gitOps.readRepoFile(
253 |         requireString(args, 0, "repoPath"),
254 |         requireString(args, 1, "filePath"),
255 |         readFileOptions(args[2]),
256 |       );
257 | 
258 |     case "git:divergence":
259 |       return gitOps.getDivergence(
260 |         requireString(args, 0, "repoPath"),
261 |         requireString(args, 1, "branch"),
262 |       );
263 | 
264 |     case "git:push":
265 |       return gitOps.gitPush(
266 |         requireString(args, 0, "repoPath"),
267 |         requireString(args, 1, "remote"),
268 |         requireString(args, 2, "branch"),
269 |       );
270 | 
271 |     case "git:pull":
272 |       return gitOps.gitPull(
273 |         requireString(args, 0, "repoPath"),
274 |         requireString(args, 1, "remote"),
275 |         requireString(args, 2, "branch"),
276 |       );
277 | 
278 |     case "git:commit":
279 |       return gitOps.gitCommit(
280 |         requireString(args, 0, "repoPath"),
281 |         requireString(args, 1, "message"),
282 |       );
283 | 
284 |     case "git:stash-pop":
285 |       return gitOps.stashPop(
286 |         requireString(args, 0, "repoPath"),
287 |         requireString(args, 1, "stashRef"),
288 |       );
289 | 
290 |     case "git:stash-drop":
291 |       return gitOps.stashDrop(
292 |         requireString(args, 0, "repoPath"),
293 |         requireString(args, 1, "stashRef"),
294 |       );
295 | 
296 |     default: {
297 |       const exhaustive: never = channel;
298 |       throw new Error(`Unknown channel: ${exhaustive}`);
299 |     }
300 |   }
301 | }
302 | 
303 | // Message handler - receives commands from main process
304 | process.parentPort?.on("message", async (message: unknown) => {
305 |   const payload = unwrapMessageData(message);
306 |   const workerMessage = isWorkerMessage(payload) ? payload : null;
307 |   const id = workerMessage?.id ?? "unknown";
308 |   try {
309 |     if (!workerMessage) {
310 |       throw new Error("Invalid worker message");
311 |     }
312 |     const result = await handleGitMessage(workerMessage);
313 |     process.parentPort?.postMessage({ id, result });
314 |   } catch (error) {
315 |     process.parentPort?.postMessage({
316 |       id,
317 |       error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : "Worker command failed",
318 |     });
319 |   }
320 | });
</content>

<content lines="1-72">
 1 | import { create } from "zustand";
 2 | 
 3 | export type Screen =
 4 |   | "dashboard"
 5 |   | "repo-detail"
 6 |   | "prs"
 7 |   | "pr-detail"
 8 |   | "issues"
 9 |   | "issue-detail"
10 |   | "repositories"
11 |   | "settings";
12 | 
13 | export interface PRDetailRef {
14 |   provider: "github" | "gitlab";
15 |   repoFullName: string;
16 |   projectId?: string;
17 |   number: number;
18 | }
19 | 
20 | export type IssueProvider = "github" | "gitlab";
21 | 
22 | export interface IssueDetailRef {
23 |   repoFullName: string;
24 |   number: number;
25 |   // `provider` defaults to "github" when omitted so existing GitHub call
26 |   // sites stay backwards-compatible. `projectId` is required for GitLab
27 |   // detail fetches because GitLab routes by numeric project id, not by
28 |   // path.
29 |   provider?: IssueProvider;
30 |   projectId?: string;
31 | }
32 | 
33 | interface NavState {
34 |   screen: Screen;
35 |   repoId: string | null;
36 |   prRef: PRDetailRef | null;
37 |   issueRepo: string | null;
38 |   issueNumber: number | null;
39 |   issueProvider: IssueProvider;
40 |   issueProjectId: string | null;
41 |   navigate: (screen: Screen, repoId?: string | null) => void;
42 |   openPRDetail: (ref: PRDetailRef) => void;
43 |   openIssueDetail: (ref: IssueDetailRef) => void;
44 |   setIssueRepo: (repoFullName: string | null) => void;
45 |   setIssueProvider: (provider: IssueProvider) => void;
46 | }
47 | 
48 | export const useNav = create<NavState>((set) => ({
49 |   screen: "dashboard",
50 |   repoId: null,
51 |   prRef: null,
52 |   issueRepo: null,
53 |   issueNumber: null,
54 |   issueProvider: "github",
55 |   issueProjectId: null,
56 |   navigate: (screen, repoId = null) => set({ screen, repoId }),
57 |   openPRDetail: (ref) => set({ screen: "pr-detail", prRef: ref }),
58 |   openIssueDetail: (ref) =>
59 |     set({
60 |       screen: "issue-detail",
61 |       issueRepo: ref.repoFullName,
62 |       issueNumber: ref.number,
63 |       issueProvider: ref.provider ?? "github",
64 |       issueProjectId: ref.projectId ?? null,
65 |     }),
66 |   setIssueRepo: (repoFullName) => set({ issueRepo: repoFullName }),
67 |   setIssueProvider: (provider) =>
68 |     // Reset the repo selection because GitHub/GitLab repo identifiers live
69 |     // in different namespaces — keeping the old value across a swap leads
70 |     // to "no issues found" with a stale picker.
71 |     set({ issueProvider: provider, issueRepo: null, issueProjectId: null }),
72 | }));
</content>

<file><path>src/store/useAIPanel.ts</path>
<content lines="1-27">
 1 | import { create } from "zustand";
 2 | import type { AIFeature, AIFeaturePayload } from "../lib/ai-features";
 3 | 
 4 | interface AIPanelState {
 5 |   isOpen: boolean;
 6 |   feature: AIFeature | null;
 7 |   payload: AIFeaturePayload | null;
 8 |   /**
 9 |    * Open a feature view inside the AI panel. `payload` is optional so the
10 |    * home view can navigate to features that gather their own context
11 |    * (e.g. issue_triage). External callers that pass a payload keep working
12 |    * unchanged — this is an additive relaxation of the signature.
13 |    */
14 |   open: (feature: AIFeature, payload?: AIFeaturePayload) => void;
15 |   close: () => void;
16 |   toggle: () => void;
17 | }
18 | 
19 | export const useAIPanel = create<AIPanelState>((set) => ({
20 |   isOpen: false,
21 |   feature: null,
22 |   payload: null,
23 |   open: (feature, payload) =>
24 |     set({ isOpen: true, feature, payload: payload ?? null }),
25 |   close: () => set({ isOpen: false, feature: null, payload: null }),
26 |   toggle: () => set((s) => ({ isOpen: !s.isOpen })),
27 | }));

<file><path>src/store/useLocalChanges.ts</path>
<content lines="1-40">
 1 | import { create } from "zustand";
 2 | 
 3 | /**
 4 |  * Right-slide panel that aggregates dirty files across all workspace repos.
 5 |  * Opens from the Dashboard "Local changes detected" stat card. The panel
 6 |  * itself owns the data fetch — this store is just the open/close hinge so
 7 |  * any surface in the app can summon it.
 8 |  *
 9 |  * Open is idempotent: calling open() while already open is a no-op for the
10 |  * store, but the panel watches `isOpen` transitions and additionally
11 |  * exposes a `refreshTick` you can bump to force a re-fetch even when the
12 |  * panel was already open.
13 |  */
14 | interface LocalChangesState {
15 |   isOpen: boolean;
16 |   /** Monotonic counter — incremented on every open() call. The panel
17 |    *  effect depends on it so a second open() while already mounted
18 |    *  still triggers a re-fetch (matches the "open is idempotent → refresh"
19 |    *  contract in the spec). */
20 |   refreshTick: number;
21 |   open: () => void;
22 |   close: () => void;
23 |   toggle: () => void;
24 | }
25 | 
26 | export const useLocalChanges = create<LocalChangesState>((set) => ({
27 |   isOpen: false,
28 |   refreshTick: 0,
29 |   open: () =>
30 |     set((state) => ({
31 |       isOpen: true,
32 |       refreshTick: state.refreshTick + 1,
33 |     })),
34 |   close: () => set({ isOpen: false }),
35 |   toggle: () =>
36 |     set((state) => ({
37 |       isOpen: !state.isOpen,
38 |       refreshTick: state.isOpen ? state.refreshTick : state.refreshTick + 1,
39 |     })),
40 | }));
</content>
</file>

  1 | // watsonx.ai Granite client. Default targets a 2026-current Granite 4 model;
  2 | // user can override per-app via Settings UI (settings.watsonx_model_id), or via
  3 | // WATSONX_MODEL_ID env. ibm/granite-3-8b-instruct was withdrawn 2026-02-22.
  4 | import * as storeLib from "./store";
  5 | 
  6 | const DEFAULT_MODEL_ID = "ibm/granite-4-h-small";
  7 | // Granite-only allowlist. The hackathon scores on watsonx.ai Granite usage,
  8 | // and showing a non-Granite model in the Settings health panel dilutes the
  9 | // attribution narrative. If you ever want to fall back to a different vendor,
 10 | // add it back here and the rest of the health-probe machinery just works.
 11 | const KNOWN_MODELS = [
 12 |   "ibm/granite-4-h-small",
 13 |   "ibm/granite-3-3-8b-instruct",
 14 |   "ibm/granite-3-2-8b-instruct",
 15 | ] as const;
 16 | const REQUIRED_ENV = [
 17 |   "WATSONX_API_KEY",
 18 |   "WATSONX_PROJECT_ID",
 19 |   "WATSONX_URL",
 20 | ] as const;
 21 | const HEALTH_CACHE_TTL_MS = 10 * 60 * 1000;
 22 | const HEALTH_PROBE_TIMEOUT_MS = 8_000;
 23 | const HEALTH_HISTORY_LIMIT = 5;
 24 | const WATSONX_API_VERSION = "2023-05-29";
 25 | 
 26 | export type RequiredWatsonxEnv = (typeof REQUIRED_ENV)[number];
 27 | export type AIEnvStatus = "configured" | "missing";
 28 | export type AIModelHealthStatus =
 29 |   | "available"
 30 |   | "unavailable"
 31 |   | "not_configured"
 32 |   | "unknown";
 33 | 
 34 | export interface AIModelHealthHistoryEntry {
 35 |   status: AIModelHealthStatus;
 36 |   checkedAt: number;
 37 |   latencyMs?: number;
 38 | }
 39 | 
 40 | export interface AIModelHealth {
 41 |   model: string;
 42 |   status: AIModelHealthStatus;
 43 |   reason?: string;
 44 |   checkedAt: number | null;
 45 |   latencyMs?: number;
 46 |   history?: AIModelHealthHistoryEntry[];
 47 | }
 48 | 
 49 | export interface AIStatus {
 50 |   configured: boolean;
 51 |   model: string;
 52 |   missing: RequiredWatsonxEnv[];
 53 |   env: Record<RequiredWatsonxEnv, AIEnvStatus>;
 54 |   health: AIModelHealth[];
 55 | }
 56 | 
 57 | let tokenCache: { token: string | null; expiresAt: number } = {
 58 |   token: null,
 59 |   expiresAt: 0,
 60 | };
 61 | 
 62 | const healthCache = new Map<
 63 |   string,
 64 |   { expiresAt: number; value: AIModelHealth }
 65 | >();
 66 | 
 67 | // Rolling per-model history of the most recent probe resolutions (cap = 5).
 68 | // Keyed by model id; oldest entry is shifted off when full.
 69 | const healthHistory = new Map<string, AIModelHealthHistoryEntry[]>();
 70 | 
 71 | function recordHealthHistory(health: AIModelHealth): AIModelHealthHistoryEntry[] {
 72 |   const list = healthHistory.get(health.model) ?? [];
 73 |   list.push({
 74 |     status: health.status,
 75 |     checkedAt: health.checkedAt ?? Date.now(),
 76 |     latencyMs: health.latencyMs,
 77 |   });
 78 |   while (list.length > HEALTH_HISTORY_LIMIT) list.shift();
 79 |   healthHistory.set(health.model, list);
 80 |   return list;
 81 | }
 82 | 
 83 | function withHistory(health: AIModelHealth): AIModelHealth {
 84 |   const list = healthHistory.get(health.model);
 85 |   return list && list.length > 0
 86 |     ? { ...health, history: list.slice() }
 87 |     : health;
 88 | }
 89 | 
 90 | export function configuredModel(): string {
 91 |   try {
 92 |     const settings = storeLib.getStoreValue("settings") as
 93 |       | { watsonx_model_id?: string }
 94 |       | undefined;
 95 |     if (settings?.watsonx_model_id && settings.watsonx_model_id.trim()) {
 96 |       return settings.watsonx_model_id.trim();
 97 |     }
 98 |   } catch {
 99 |     // Settings unreadable — fall through to env / default.
100 |   }
101 |   return process.env.WATSONX_MODEL_ID?.trim() || DEFAULT_MODEL_ID;
102 | }
103 | 
104 | function envValue(name: RequiredWatsonxEnv): string | undefined {
105 |   const value = process.env[name]?.trim();
106 |   return value || undefined;
107 | }
108 | 
109 | function envStatus(): {
110 |   missing: RequiredWatsonxEnv[];
111 |   env: Record<RequiredWatsonxEnv, AIEnvStatus>;
112 | } {
113 |   const missing: RequiredWatsonxEnv[] = [];
114 |   const env = {} as Record<RequiredWatsonxEnv, AIEnvStatus>;
115 |   for (const name of REQUIRED_ENV) {
116 |     const configured = !!envValue(name);
117 |     env[name] = configured ? "configured" : "missing";
118 |     if (!configured) missing.push(name);
119 |   }
120 |   return { missing, env };
121 | }
122 | 
123 | function watsonxBaseUrl(): string | undefined {
124 |   return envValue("WATSONX_URL")?.replace(/\/+$/, "");
125 | }
126 | 
127 | export async function aiConfigStatus(): Promise<AIStatus> {
128 |   const { missing, env } = envStatus();
129 |   const model = configuredModel();
130 |   const configured = missing.length === 0;
131 |   return {
132 |     configured,
133 |     model,
134 |     missing,
135 |     env,
136 |     health: await modelHealthEntries(configured, missing, model),
137 |   };
138 | }
139 | 
140 | async function getIAMToken(): Promise<string> {
141 |   if (tokenCache.token && Date.now() < tokenCache.expiresAt - 600_000) {
142 |     return tokenCache.token;
143 |   }
144 | 
145 |   const apiKey = envValue("WATSONX_API_KEY");
146 |   if (!apiKey) {
147 |     throw new Error("WATSONX_API_KEY missing from .env");
148 |   }
149 | 
150 |   const tokenBody = new URLSearchParams({
151 |     grant_type: "urn:ibm:params:oauth:grant-type:apikey",
152 |     apikey: apiKey,
153 |   });
154 |   const response = await fetch("https://iam.cloud.ibm.com/identity/token", {
155 |     method: "POST",
156 |     headers: {
157 |       "Content-Type": "application/x-www-form-urlencoded",
158 |     },
159 |     body: tokenBody,
160 |   });
161 | 
162 |   if (!response.ok) {
163 |     throw new Error(
164 |       `IAM token request failed: ${response.status} ${response.statusText}`,
165 |     );
166 |   }
167 | 
168 |   const data = await response.json();
169 |   if (!data.access_token) {
170 |     throw new Error("IAM response missing access_token");
171 |   }
172 |   tokenCache = {
173 |     token: data.access_token,
174 |     expiresAt: (data.expiration ?? 0) * 1000,
175 |   };
176 | 
177 |   return data.access_token;
178 | }
179 | 
180 | function uniqueModels(activeModel: string): string[] {
181 |   return Array.from(new Set([...KNOWN_MODELS, activeModel]));
182 | }
183 | 
184 | function notConfiguredHealth(
185 |   model: string,
186 |   missing: RequiredWatsonxEnv[],
187 | ): AIModelHealth {
188 |   return {
189 |     model,
190 |     status: "not_configured",
191 |     reason: `Missing ${missing.join(", ")}`,
192 |     checkedAt: null,
193 |   };
194 | }
195 | 
196 | function unknownHealth(
197 |   model: string,
198 |   reason: string,
199 |   checkedAt: number,
200 | ): AIModelHealth {
201 |   return {
202 |     model,
203 |     status: "unknown",
204 |     reason,
205 |     checkedAt,
206 |   };
207 | }
208 | 
209 | async function modelHealthEntries(
210 |   configured: boolean,
211 |   missing: RequiredWatsonxEnv[],
212 |   activeModel: string,
213 | ): Promise<AIModelHealth[]> {
214 |   const models = uniqueModels(activeModel);
215 |   if (!configured) {
216 |     return models.map((model) => notConfiguredHealth(model, missing));
217 |   }
218 | 
219 |   const checkedAt = Date.now();
220 |   const healthByModel = new Map<string, AIModelHealth>();
221 |   const modelsToProbe: string[] = [];
222 |   for (const model of models) {
223 |     const cached = healthCache.get(model);
224 |     if (cached && cached.expiresAt > checkedAt) {
225 |       healthByModel.set(model, cached.value);
226 |     } else {
227 |       modelsToProbe.push(model);
228 |     }
229 |   }
230 | 
231 |   if (modelsToProbe.length === 0) {
232 |     return orderedHealthEntries(models, healthByModel, checkedAt);
233 |   }
234 | 
235 |   let token: string;
236 |   try {
237 |     token = await getIAMToken();
238 |   } catch (error) {
239 |     const reason = sanitizeProbeError(error);
240 |     for (const model of modelsToProbe) {
241 |       const health = unknownHealth(model, reason, checkedAt);
242 |       recordHealthHistory(health);
243 |       healthByModel.set(model, health);
244 |       healthCache.set(model, {
245 |         value: health,
246 |         expiresAt: checkedAt + HEALTH_CACHE_TTL_MS,
247 |       });
248 |     }
249 |     return orderedHealthEntries(models, healthByModel, checkedAt);
250 |   }
251 | 
252 |   const probed = await Promise.all(
253 |     modelsToProbe.map((model) => probeAndCacheModel(model, token, checkedAt)),
254 |   );
255 |   for (const health of probed) {
256 |     healthByModel.set(health.model, health);
257 |   }
258 |   return orderedHealthEntries(models, healthByModel, checkedAt);
259 | }
260 | 
261 | function orderedHealthEntries(
262 |   models: string[],
263 |   healthByModel: Map<string, AIModelHealth>,
264 |   checkedAt: number,
265 | ): AIModelHealth[] {
266 |   return models.map((model) =>
267 |     withHistory(
268 |       healthByModel.get(model) ??
269 |         unknownHealth(model, "Health probe failed", checkedAt),
270 |     ),
271 |   );
272 | }
273 | 
274 | async function probeAndCacheModel(
275 |   model: string,
276 |   token: string,
277 |   checkedAt: number,
278 | ): Promise<AIModelHealth> {
279 |   const value = await probeModel(model, token, checkedAt);
280 |   recordHealthHistory(value);
281 |   healthCache.set(model, {
282 |     value,
283 |     expiresAt: checkedAt + HEALTH_CACHE_TTL_MS,
284 |   });
285 |   return value;
286 | }
287 | 
288 | async function probeModel(
289 |   model: string,
290 |   token: string,
291 |   checkedAt: number,
292 | ): Promise<AIModelHealth> {
293 |   const baseUrl = watsonxBaseUrl();
294 |   const projectId = envValue("WATSONX_PROJECT_ID");
295 |   if (!baseUrl || !projectId) {
296 |     return unknownHealth(
297 |       model,
298 |       "watsonx.ai configuration is incomplete",
299 |       checkedAt,
300 |     );
301 |   }
302 | 
303 |   const controller = new AbortController();
304 |   const timeout = setTimeout(() => controller.abort(), HEALTH_PROBE_TIMEOUT_MS);
305 |   const startedAt = Date.now();
306 |   try {
307 |     const response = await fetch(
308 |       `${baseUrl}/ml/v1/chat/completions?version=${WATSONX_API_VERSION}`,
309 |       {
310 |         method: "POST",
311 |         signal: controller.signal,
312 |         headers: {
313 |           Authorization: `Bearer ${token}`,
314 |           "Content-Type": "application/json",
315 |           Accept: "application/json",
316 |         },
317 |         body: JSON.stringify({
318 |           model,
319 |           project_id: projectId,
320 |           messages: [{ role: "user", content: "health check" }],
321 |           max_tokens: 1,
322 |           temperature: 0,
323 |         }),
324 |       },
325 |     );
326 |     await discardBody(response);
327 |     const latencyMs = Date.now() - startedAt;
328 |     if (response.ok) {
329 |       return { model, status: "available", checkedAt, latencyMs };
330 |     }
331 |     return {
332 |       model,
333 |       status: "unavailable",
334 |       reason: sanitizeProbeHttpStatus(response.status),
335 |       checkedAt,
336 |       latencyMs,
337 |     };
338 |   } catch (error) {
339 |     const latencyMs = Date.now() - startedAt;
340 |     return {
341 |       ...unknownHealth(model, sanitizeProbeError(error), checkedAt),
342 |       latencyMs,
343 |     };
344 |   } finally {
345 |     clearTimeout(timeout);
346 |   }
347 | }
348 | 
349 | async function discardBody(response: Response): Promise<void> {
350 |   try {
351 |     await response.arrayBuffer();
352 |   } catch {
353 |     // Health checks only need the status code; response bodies are intentionally ignored.
354 |   }
355 | }
356 | 
357 | function sanitizeProbeHttpStatus(status: number): string {
358 |   if (status === 400) return "Model probe was rejected";
359 |   if (status === 401 || status === 403) return "watsonx.ai credentials rejected";
360 |   if (status === 404) return "Model is not available for this project";
361 |   if (status === 429) return "watsonx.ai rate limit reached";
362 |   if (status >= 500) return "watsonx.ai service error";
363 |   return `watsonx.ai returned HTTP ${status}`;
364 | }
365 | 
366 | function sanitizeProbeError(error: unknown): string {
367 |   if (error instanceof Error) {
368 |     if (error.name === "AbortError") return "Probe timed out";
369 |     const message = error.message.toLowerCase();
370 |     if (message.includes("iam token request failed")) {
371 |       return "IAM token request failed";
372 |     }
373 |     if (message.includes("missing")) {
374 |       return "watsonx.ai configuration is incomplete";
375 |     }
376 |     if (message.includes("fetch") || message.includes("network")) {
377 |       return "Network request failed";
378 |     }
379 |   }
380 |   return "Health probe failed";
381 | }
382 | 
383 | export async function callGranite(
384 |   systemPrompt: string,
385 |   userPrompt: string,
386 | ): Promise<string> {
387 |   const WATSONX_URL = watsonxBaseUrl();
388 |   const WATSONX_PROJECT_ID = envValue("WATSONX_PROJECT_ID");
389 |   const modelId = configuredModel();
390 | 
391 |   if (!WATSONX_URL || !WATSONX_PROJECT_ID) {
392 |     throw new Error("WATSONX_URL or WATSONX_PROJECT_ID missing from .env");
393 |   }
394 | 
395 |   const token = await getIAMToken();
396 | 
397 |   try {
398 |     const chatResult = await callGraniteChat(
399 |       WATSONX_URL,
400 |       WATSONX_PROJECT_ID,
401 |       modelId,
402 |       token,
403 |       systemPrompt,
404 |       userPrompt,
405 |     );
406 |     if (chatResult.trim()) return chatResult;
407 |   } catch (error) {
408 |     if (!isRecoverableChatFailure(error)) throw error;
409 |   }
410 | 
411 |   return callGraniteTextGeneration(
412 |     WATSONX_URL,
413 |     WATSONX_PROJECT_ID,
414 |     modelId,
415 |     token,
416 |     systemPrompt,
417 |     userPrompt,
418 |   );
419 | }
420 | 
421 | async function callGraniteChat(
422 |   WATSONX_URL: string,
423 |   WATSONX_PROJECT_ID: string,
424 |   modelId: string,
425 |   token: string,
426 |   systemPrompt: string,
427 |   userPrompt: string,
428 | ): Promise<string> {
429 |   const response = await fetch(
430 |     `${WATSONX_URL}/ml/v1/chat/completions?version=${WATSONX_API_VERSION}`,
431 |     {
432 |       method: "POST",
433 |       headers: {
434 |         Authorization: `Bearer ${token}`,
435 |         "Content-Type": "application/json",
436 |         Accept: "application/json",
437 |       },
438 |       body: JSON.stringify({
439 |         model: modelId,
440 |         project_id: WATSONX_PROJECT_ID,
441 |         messages: [
442 |           { role: "system", content: systemPrompt },
443 |           { role: "user", content: userPrompt },
444 |         ],
445 |         max_tokens: 800,
446 |         temperature: 0,
447 |       }),
448 |     },
449 |   );
450 | 
451 |   if (!response.ok) {
452 |     throw new Error(
453 |       `watsonx.ai (${modelId}) returned ${response.status} ${response.statusText}`,
454 |     );
455 |   }
456 | 
457 |   const data = await response.json();
458 |   const generated = extractChatContent(data);
459 |   if (typeof generated !== "string") {
460 |     throw new Error("watsonx.ai chat returned an unexpected payload shape");
461 |   }
462 |   return generated;
463 | }
464 | 
465 | async function callGraniteTextGeneration(
466 |   WATSONX_URL: string,
467 |   WATSONX_PROJECT_ID: string,
468 |   modelId: string,
469 |   token: string,
470 |   systemPrompt: string,
471 |   userPrompt: string,
472 | ): Promise<string> {
473 |   const response = await fetch(
474 |     `${WATSONX_URL}/ml/v1/text/generation?version=${WATSONX_API_VERSION}`,
475 |     {
476 |       method: "POST",
477 |       headers: {
478 |         Authorization: `Bearer ${token}`,
479 |         "Content-Type": "application/json",
480 |         Accept: "application/json",
481 |       },
482 |       body: JSON.stringify({
483 |         model_id: modelId,
484 |         project_id: WATSONX_PROJECT_ID,
485 |         input: `${systemPrompt}\n\n${userPrompt}`,
486 |         parameters: {
487 |           decoding_method: "greedy",
488 |           max_new_tokens: 800,
489 |           repetition_penalty: 1.05,
490 |         },
491 |       }),
492 |     },
493 |   );
494 | 
495 |   if (!response.ok) {
496 |     throw new Error(
497 |       `watsonx.ai (${modelId}) returned ${response.status} ${response.statusText}`,
498 |     );
499 |   }
500 | 
501 |   const data = await response.json();
502 |   const generated = data?.results?.[0]?.generated_text;
503 |   if (typeof generated !== "string") {
504 |     throw new Error("watsonx.ai returned an unexpected payload shape");
505 |   }
506 |   return generated;
507 | }
508 | 
509 | function extractChatContent(data: unknown): string | undefined {
510 |   const choice = (data as { choices?: Array<{ message?: { content?: unknown } }> })
511 |     ?.choices?.[0];
512 |   const content = choice?.message?.content;
513 |   if (typeof content === "string") return content;
514 |   if (Array.isArray(content)) {
515 |     return content
516 |       .map((part) =>
517 |         part && typeof part === "object" && "text" in part
518 |           ? String((part as { text: unknown }).text)
519 |           : "",
520 |       )
521 |       .filter(Boolean)
522 |       .join("\n");
523 |   }
524 |   return undefined;
525 | }
526 | 
527 | function isRecoverableChatFailure(error: unknown): boolean {
528 |   if (!(error instanceof Error)) return false;
529 |   const message = error.message.toLowerCase();
530 |   return (
531 |     message.includes("400") ||
532 |     message.includes("404") ||
533 |     message.includes("not found") ||
534 |     message.includes("unexpected payload shape")
535 |   );
536 | }
</content>

272 | export async function listRepos(token: string): Promise<GitHubRepo[]> {
273 |   const repos = await githubPaginated<GitHubRepoResponse>(
274 |     token,
275 |     "/user/repos?per_page=100&sort=updated",
276 |   );
277 |   return repos.map((repo) => ({
278 |     id: repo.id,
279 |     name: repo.name,
280 |     full_name: repo.full_name,
281 |     default_branch: repo.default_branch,
282 |     updated_at: repo.updated_at,
283 |     html_url: repo.html_url,
284 |   }));
285 | }

287 | export async function listIssues(
288 |   token: string,
289 |   owner: string,
290 |   repo: string,
291 | ): Promise<GitHubIssue[]> {
292 |   const repoFullName = `${owner}/${repo}`;
293 |   const issues = await githubPaginated<GitHubIssueResponse>(
294 |     token,
295 |     `/repos/${owner}/${repo}/issues?state=all&sort=updated&direction=desc&per_page=100`,
296 |   );
297 |   return issues
298 |     .filter((issue) => !issue.pull_request)
299 |     .map((issue) => mapIssue(issue, repoFullName));
300 | }
301 | 
302 | export async function listUserIssues(token: string): Promise<GitHubIssue[]> {
303 |   const issues = await githubPaginated<GitHubIssueResponse>(
304 |     token,
305 |     "/issues?filter=all&state=all&sort=updated&direction=desc&per_page=100",
306 |   );
307 |   return issues
308 |     .filter((issue) => !issue.pull_request)
309 |     .map((issue) => mapIssue(issue, readIssueRepoFullName(issue)));
310 | }

312 | export async function listPRs(
313 |   token: string,

315 |   repo: string,
316 | ): Promise<GitHubPR[]> {
317 |   const prs = await githubPaginated<GitHubPullResponse>(

320 |   );

323 |     title: pr.title,
324 |     author: pr.user?.login ?? "unknown",
325 |     head: pr.head?.ref ?? "",
326 |     base: pr.base?.ref ?? "",
327 |     updated_at: pr.updated_at,
328 |     html_url: pr.html_url,
329 |     draft: !!pr.draft,
330 |   }));
331 | }

333 | export async function listPipelineRuns(
334 |   token: string,
335 |   owner: string,
336 |   repo: string,
337 | ): Promise<GitHubRun[]> {
338 |   const runs = await githubPaginated<GitHubRunResponse>(
339 |     token,
340 |     `/repos/${owner}/${repo}/actions/runs?per_page=100`,
341 |     (value) => readArrayProperty<GitHubRunResponse>(value, "workflow_runs"),
342 |     5,
343 |   );
344 |   return runs.map((run) => ({
345 |     id: run.id,
346 |     name: run.name ?? null,
347 |     status: run.status ?? null,
348 |     conclusion: run.conclusion ?? null,
349 |     head_sha: run.head_sha ?? "",
350 |     head_branch: run.head_branch ?? null,
351 |     html_url: run.html_url,
352 |     updated_at: run.updated_at ?? null,
353 |   }));

356 | export async function commentOnPR(
357 |   token: string,
358 |   owner: string,
359 |   repo: string,
360 |   prNumber: number,
361 |   body: string,
362 | ): Promise<void> {
363 |   await requestVoid(
364 |     "github",
365 |     `${BASE}/repos/${owner}/${repo}/issues/${prNumber}/comments`,
366 |     {
367 |       method: "POST",
368 |       headers: {
369 |         ...authHeaders(token),
370 |         "Content-Type": "application/json",
371 |       },
372 |       body: JSON.stringify({ body }),
373 |     },
374 |   );
375 | }
376 | 
377 | export function parseFullName(fullName: string): { owner: string; repo: string } {
378 |   const trimmed = fullName.trim();
379 |   const parts = trimmed.split("/");
380 |   const segmentPattern = /^[A-Za-z0-9_.-]{1,100}$/;
381 |   if (
382 |     parts.length !== 2 ||
383 |     !segmentPattern.test(parts[0]) ||
384 |     !segmentPattern.test(parts[1]) ||
385 |     parts.some((part) => part === "." || part === ".." || part.startsWith("-"))
386 |   ) {
387 |     throw new Error("Repository name must be a valid owner/repo pair.");
388 |   }
389 |   const [owner, repo] = parts;
390 |   return { owner, repo };
391 | }
392 | 
393 | export async function fetchIssueDetail(
394 |   token: string,
395 |   owner: string,
396 |   repo: string,
397 |   issueNumber: number,
398 | ): Promise<GitHubIssueDetail> {
399 |   const [issue, comments, timeline] = await Promise.all([
400 |     githubJson<GitHubIssueResponse>(token, `/repos/${owner}/${repo}/issues/${issueNumber}`),
401 |     githubPaginated<GitHubCommentResponse>(
402 |       token,
403 |       `/repos/${owner}/${repo}/issues/${issueNumber}/comments?per_page=100`,
404 |     ),
405 |     githubPaginated<unknown>(
406 |       token,
407 |       `/repos/${owner}/${repo}/issues/${issueNumber}/timeline?per_page=100`,
408 |     ).catch(() => []),
409 |   ]);
410 | 
411 |   if (issue.pull_request) {
412 |     throw new Error(`GitHub #${issueNumber} is a pull request, not an issue.`);
413 |   }
414 | 
415 |   return {
416 |     repoFullName: `${owner}/${repo}`,
417 |     number: issue.number,
418 |     title: issue.title,
419 |     author: issue.user?.login ?? "unknown",
420 |     state: issue.state,
421 |     labels: mapIssueLabels(issue.labels),
422 |     assignees: issue.assignees?.map((assignee) => assignee.login ?? "").filter(Boolean) ?? [],
423 |     comments: issue.comments,
424 |     updated_at: issue.updated_at,
425 |     html_url: issue.html_url,
426 |     body: issue.body ?? "",
427 |     locked: !!issue.locked,
428 |     milestone: mapMilestoneSummary(issue.milestone),
429 |     commentsData: comments.map(mapComment),
430 |     linkedPullRequests: mapTimelineLinkedPRs(timeline),
431 |   };
432 | }
433 | 
434 | export async function fetchPRDetail(
435 |   token: string,
436 |   owner: string,
437 |   repo: string,
438 |   prNumber: number,
439 | ): Promise<PullRequestDetail> {
440 |   const [pr, files, commits, issueComments, reviewComments, reviews, checks] =
441 |     await Promise.all([
442 |       githubJson<GitHubPullResponse>(token, `/repos/${owner}/${repo}/pulls/${prNumber}`),
443 |       githubPaginated<GitHubFileResponse>(
444 |         token,
445 |         `/repos/${owner}/${repo}/pulls/${prNumber}/files?per_page=100`,
446 |       ),
447 |       githubPaginated<GitHubCommitResponse>(
448 |         token,
449 |         `/repos/${owner}/${repo}/pulls/${prNumber}/commits?per_page=100`,
450 |       ),
451 |       githubPaginated<GitHubCommentResponse>(
452 |         token,
453 |         `/repos/${owner}/${repo}/issues/${prNumber}/comments?per_page=100`,
454 |       ),
455 |       githubPaginated<GitHubCommentResponse>(
456 |         token,
457 |         `/repos/${owner}/${repo}/pulls/${prNumber}/comments?per_page=100`,
458 |       ),
459 |       githubPaginated<GitHubReviewResponse>(
460 |         token,
461 |         `/repos/${owner}/${repo}/pulls/${prNumber}/reviews?per_page=100`,
462 |       ),
463 |       githubPaginated<GitHubCheckRunResponse>(
464 |         token,
465 |         `/repos/${owner}/${repo}/commits/pull/${prNumber}/head/check-runs?per_page=100`,
466 |         (value) => readArrayProperty<GitHubCheckRunResponse>(value, "check_runs"),
467 |         5,
468 |       ).catch(() => []),
469 |     ]);
470 | 
471 |   return {
472 |     id: `github:${owner}/${repo}:${prNumber}`,
473 |     provider: "github",
474 |     repoFullName: `${owner}/${repo}`,
475 |     number: prNumber,
476 |     numberPrefix: "#",
477 |     title: pr.title,
478 |     body: pr.body ?? "",
479 |     author: pr.user?.login ?? "unknown",
480 |     source_branch: pr.head?.ref ?? "",
481 |     target_branch: pr.base?.ref ?? "",
482 |     status: pr.merged
483 |       ? "merged"
484 |       : pr.state === "closed"
485 |         ? "closed"
486 |         : pr.draft
487 |           ? "draft"
488 |           : "open",
489 |     draft: !!pr.draft,
490 |     url: pr.html_url,
491 |     updated_at: pr.updated_at,
492 |     files: files.map((file) => ({
493 |       path: file.filename,
494 |       status: mapFileStatus(file.status),
495 |       additions: file.additions ?? 0,
496 |       deletions: file.deletions ?? 0,
497 |       patch: file.patch,
498 |       previous_path: file.previous_filename,
499 |     })),
500 |     commits: commits.map((commit) => ({
501 |       sha: commit.sha,
502 |       message: commit.commit?.message ?? "",
503 |       author: commit.author?.login || commit.commit?.author?.name || "unknown",
504 |       date: commit.commit?.author?.date || commit.commit?.committer?.date || "",
505 |       url: commit.html_url,
506 |     })),
507 |     comments: issueComments.map(mapComment),
508 |     reviewComments: reviewComments.map((comment) => ({
509 |       ...mapComment(comment),
510 |       file_path: comment.path,
511 |       line: comment.line ?? comment.original_line ?? undefined,
512 |     })),
513 |     reviews: reviews.map((review) => ({
514 |       id: String(review.id),
515 |       author: review.user?.login ?? "unknown",
516 |       body: `[${review.state}] ${review.body ?? ""}`.trim(),
517 |       created_at: review.submitted_at ?? "",
518 |       url: review.html_url,
519 |     })),
520 |     checks: checks.map((run) => ({
521 |       id: String(run.id),
522 |       name: run.name,
523 |       status: run.status,
524 |       conclusion: run.conclusion,
525 |       url: run.html_url ?? undefined,
526 |       updated_at: run.completed_at ?? run.started_at,
527 |     })),
528 |   };
529 | }
530 | 
531 | function githubJson<T>(token: string, path: string): Promise<T> {
532 |   return requestJson<T>("github", `${BASE}${path}`, {
533 |     headers: authHeaders(token),
534 |   });
535 | }
536 | 
537 | function githubPaginated<T>(
538 |   token: string,
539 |   path: string,
540 |   extractItems?: (value: unknown) => T[],
541 |   maxPages = 10,
542 | ): Promise<T[]> {
543 |   return requestPaginated<T>(
544 |     "github",
545 |     `${BASE}${path}`,
546 |     { headers: authHeaders(token) },
547 |     { extractItems, maxPages },
548 |   );
549 | }
550 | 
551 | function mapComment(comment: GitHubCommentResponse): ReviewThreadItem {
552 |   return {
553 |     id: String(comment.id),
554 |     author: comment.user?.login ?? "unknown",
555 |     body: comment.body ?? "",
556 |     created_at: comment.created_at,
557 |     updated_at: comment.updated_at,
558 |     url: comment.html_url,
559 |   };
560 | }
561 | 
562 | function mapIssue(issue: GitHubIssueResponse, repoFullName: string): GitHubIssue {
563 |   return {
564 |     repoFullName,
565 |     number: issue.number,
566 |     title: issue.title,
567 |     author: issue.user?.login ?? "unknown",
568 |     state: issue.state,
569 |     labels: mapIssueLabels(issue.labels),
570 |     assignees: issue.assignees?.map((assignee) => assignee.login ?? "").filter(Boolean) ?? [],
571 |     comments: issue.comments,
572 |     updated_at: issue.updated_at,
573 |     html_url: issue.html_url,
574 |   };
575 | }
576 | 
577 | function mapMilestoneSummary(
578 |   milestone: GitHubIssueResponse["milestone"],
579 | ): GitHubMilestoneSummary | null {
580 |   if (!milestone) return null;
581 |   const title = milestone.title?.trim();
582 |   if (!title) return null;
583 |   const summary: GitHubMilestoneSummary = { title };
584 |   if (typeof milestone.open_issues === "number") {
585 |     summary.openIssues = milestone.open_issues;
586 |   }
587 |   if (typeof milestone.closed_issues === "number") {
588 |     summary.closedIssues = milestone.closed_issues;
589 |   }
590 |   if (typeof milestone.due_on === "string" && milestone.due_on.length > 0) {
591 |     summary.dueOn = milestone.due_on;
592 |   }
593 |   return summary;
594 | }
595 | 
596 | function readIssueRepoFullName(issue: GitHubIssueResponse): string {
597 |   if (issue.repository?.full_name) return issue.repository.full_name;
598 |   const match = /^https:\/\/github\.com\/([^/]+\/[^/]+)\//.exec(issue.html_url);
599 |   return match?.[1] ?? "unknown/unknown";
600 | }
601 | 
602 | function mapIssueLabels(labels: unknown[]): GitHubIssueLabel[] {
603 |   return labels
604 |     .map((label) => {
605 |       if (typeof label === "string") {
606 |         return { name: label, color: null, description: null };
607 |       }
608 |       if (!label || typeof label !== "object") return null;
609 |       const item = label as {
610 |         name?: unknown;
611 |         color?: unknown;
612 |         description?: unknown;
613 |       };
614 |       const name = typeof item.name === "string" ? item.name : "";
615 |       if (!name) return null;
616 |       return {
617 |         name,
618 |         color: typeof item.color === "string" ? item.color : null,
619 |         description: typeof item.description === "string" ? item.description : null,
620 |       };
621 |     })
622 |     .filter((label): label is GitHubIssueLabel => label !== null);
623 | }
624 | 
625 | function mapTimelineLinkedPRs(events: unknown[]): GitHubLinkedPullRequest[] {
626 |   const byNumber = new Map<number, GitHubLinkedPullRequest>();
627 |   for (const event of events) {
628 |     if (!event || typeof event !== "object") continue;
629 |     const source = (event as { source?: unknown }).source;
630 |     if (!source || typeof source !== "object") continue;
631 |     const issue = (source as { issue?: unknown }).issue;
632 |     if (!issue || typeof issue !== "object") continue;
633 |     const candidate = issue as {
634 |       number?: unknown;
635 |       title?: unknown;
636 |       state?: unknown;
637 |       html_url?: unknown;
638 |       pull_request?: unknown;
639 |     };
640 |     if (!candidate.pull_request || typeof candidate.number !== "number") continue;
641 |     byNumber.set(candidate.number, {
642 |       number: candidate.number,
643 |       title: typeof candidate.title === "string" ? candidate.title : "",
644 |       state: typeof candidate.state === "string" ? candidate.state : "unknown",
645 |       url: typeof candidate.html_url === "string" ? candidate.html_url : "",
646 |     });
647 |   }
648 |   return Array.from(byNumber.values()).sort((a, b) => a.number - b.number);
649 | }
650 | 
651 | function mapFileStatus(status: string): PullRequestFile["status"] {
652 |   switch (status) {
653 |     case "added":
654 |     case "modified":
655 |     case "removed":
656 |     case "renamed":
657 |       return status;
658 |     default:
659 |       return "unknown";
660 |   }
661 | }
662 | 
663 | function readArrayProperty<T>(value: unknown, property: string): T[] {
664 |   if (!value || typeof value !== "object") return [];
665 |   const items = (value as Record<string, unknown>)[property];
666 |   return Array.isArray(items) ? (items as T[]) : [];
667 | }
</content>

  1 | import type {
  2 |   GitHubIssue,
  3 |   GitHubIssueDetail,

  9 |   PullRequestFile,

 12 | import {
 13 |   requestJson,
 14 |   requestPaginated,
 15 |   requestVoid,
 16 | } from "./provider-http";
 17 | 
 18 | // GitLab issue summaries and details conform to the same shape used by the
 19 | // GitHub backend (see `GitHubIssue` / `GitHubIssueDetail`), so the UI can be
 20 | // provider-agnostic. We re-export those names as `GitLabIssue` /
 21 | // `GitLabIssueDetail` for read-site clarity in the IPC layer.
 22 | export type GitLabIssue = GitHubIssue;
 23 | export type GitLabIssueDetail = GitHubIssueDetail;
 24 | 
 25 | const BASE = "https://gitlab.com/api/v4";
 26 | 
 27 | function authHeaders(token: string): HeadersInit {
 28 |   return {
 29 |     Authorization: `Bearer ${token}`,
 30 |     Accept: "application/json",
 31 |   };
 32 | }

 38 |   default_branch: string | null;
 39 |   web_url: string;
 40 |   last_activity_at: string;
 41 | }

 91 |   web_url: string;

 93 | }

194 | export async function listProjects(token: string): Promise<GitLabProject[]> {
195 |   const data = await gitlabPaginated<GitLabProjectResponse>(
196 |     token,
197 |     "/projects?membership=true&per_page=100&order_by=last_activity_at",
198 |   );
199 |   return data.map((project) => ({
200 |     id: project.id,
201 |     name: project.name,
202 |     path_with_namespace: project.path_with_namespace,
203 |     default_branch: project.default_branch,
204 |     web_url: project.web_url,
205 |     last_activity_at: project.last_activity_at,
206 |   }));
